Introducing Sharh al-Nazair: A Commentary on Hanafi Legal Maxims
Title page of a Hanafi legal maxim commentary

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the source and significance of Sharh al-Nazair as a key text in the Hanafi usul al-iftaa tradition.

Core Idea
Sharh al-Nazair unlocks Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair — the authoritative Hanafi work on legal maxims.

This title page marks the beginning of Sharh al-Nazair, an Urdu commentary on the classic Hanafi text Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair by Ibn Nujaym. This work is essential for understanding the qawaid kulliya (legal maxims) that underpin Hanafi fatwa methodology. The Quranic verse quoted calls for deep reflection, fitting for a text that trains the mufti in applying principles.

Guided Path
1
Identify the book and its subject
Recognize that Sharh al-Nazair is a commentary on Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair, a foundational work on Hanafi legal maxims (qawaid kulliya).
2
Place it in the tradition
Understand that this text is part of the usul al-iftaa corpus, essential for deriving fatwas from principles rather than from individual rulings.

Commentary
This passage is the title page of the Urdu commentary on Ibn Nujaym's Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair, a foundational Hanafi work on legal maxims (qawaid kulliya). The commentator, Mufti Muhammad Mas'um al-Qasimi, is a contemporary scholar of Hadith and a professor at a madrasa in Manglore, Uttarakhand. The book is published by Maktabah al-Arif in Deoband. The verse quoted (Quran 59:2) encourages reflection, fitting for a work on usul al-iftaa and qawaid.

Introduction to Sharah al-Nazair: The 19 Qawa'id of Hanafi Iftaa
Title page and TOC of a Hanafi maxims commentary

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the structure and purpose of Sharah al-Nazair and state the number and role of the 19 major qawa'id in Hanafi iftaa.

Core Idea
The 19 major qawa'id of Ibn Nujaym form the backbone of Hanafi fatwa derivation.

This lesson introduces Sharah al-Nazair, an Urdu commentary on Ibn Nujaym's al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Mufti Muhammad Mas'um al-Qasimi. The table of contents lists 19 major qawa'id, which are the foundational legal maxims of Hanafi fiqh. Understanding this structure is the first step to mastering Hanafi iftaa methodology.

Guided Path
1
Identify the book's purpose
Examine the title and author information. The book is a commentary (sharah) on al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir, a classic work on Hanafi legal maxims. The purpose is to explain and apply these maxims for fatwa derivation.
The Quranic verse at the start is an admonition to reflect, not part of the title.
2
Recognize the importance of qawa'id
Qawa'id are general principles that encompass many specific rulings. In Hanafi iftaa, they ensure consistency when faced with new cases.
The 19 maxims here are the major kubra maxims.
3
List the 19 qawa'id
From the table of contents, note the numbered maxims from first to nineteenth. This list is the core content of the book.
The twelfth entry is simply 'قواعد' (maxims), possibly a subheading.
4
Relate to the original al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir
Understand that this is a commentary, so each maxim will be explained with examples and applications from Hanafi sources.
The original work by Ibn Nujaym is a foundational text in Hanafi usul al-iftā.

Commentary
This passage is front matter from the Urdu commentary on Ibn Nujaym's al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir. It begins with a Quranic verse (likely 59:2) calling for reflection. The book title 'Sharah al-Nazair' indicates it is a commentary on legal maxims and similar cases. The commentator is Mufti Muhammad Mas'um al-Qasimi, a teacher at an Islamic seminary in Mangaluru, India. The publisher is Maktabatul Arif Deoband. The table of contents lists nineteen 'qawa'id' (maxims), which are the core of the work. This tells us that the book covers all the major kubra maxims of Hanafi fiqh, arranged systematically. In the Hanafi tradition, such maxims (qawa'id kulliya) serve as foundational principles from which many furu' (branch rulings) are derived. The list includes up to the nineteenth maxim; note that the twelfth entry is simply 'قواعد' (maxims) perhaps as a subheading. The user of this book should expect detailed discussions of each maxim with applications.

Key Terms
قاعدة (qa'idah): A legal maxim that encompasses many related fiqh rulings under a single principle.
شرح (sharah): A commentary that explains and expands upon a base text.
الأشباه والنظائر (al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir): The title of Ibn Nujaym's seminal work on Hanafi legal maxims.

Key Terms from Source Passage

An Overview of the Nineteen Legal Maxims (Qawaid)
Listing the nineteen qawaid as a table of contents

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to list the nineteen qawaid and explain their role in Hanafi iftaa.

Core Idea
The nineteen qawaid are the foundational principles that govern Hanafi fatwa derivation.

This passage is the book's table of contents (fihrist), listing the nineteen qawaid (legal maxims) that form the core of this work. As a mufti, mastering these maxims is essential for consistent and principled fatwa-giving. This lesson introduces the overall structure and significance of these qawaid.

Guided Path
1
Identify the total count
Count the number of entries from 'al-qa'ida al-ula' to 'al-qa'ida al-tasi'a 'ashar'. There are 19.
Do not include the standalone 'qawa'id' line as a separate maxim.
2
Recognize the numbering pattern
Note that Arabic ordinals are used and that the word 'qawa'id' appears before the thirteenth rule, possibly marking a subsection.
This may indicate a new section or a summary.
3
Understand the purpose of the fihrist
This list provides the roadmap for the entire book; each qa'ida will be explained with its applications in later lessons.
4
Connect to the discipline of iftaa
Appreciate that these qawaid are tools for a mufti to derive consistent rulings across various fiqh chapters.
Memorizing the names and order is the first step toward applying them.

The numbering runs from al-qa'ida al-ula (first rule) to al-qa'ida al-tasi'a 'ashar (nineteenth rule). There is also a line stating 'qawa'id' (rules) before the thirteenth rule, which may indicate a section heading. This fihrist provides an overview of the structure of the book.

The Pedagogy of Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair: Lessons from a Taqriz
Praise for a commentary and discussion of teaching methodology

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain why the effective teaching of Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair requires a teacher skilled in istinbat and practical exercises, and identify the implications for ifta training.

Core Idea
Teaching Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair without istinbat practice is like a dead text; the teacher must be a living exponent of deduction.

This taqriz (endorsement) by Khatib al-Islam Muhammad Salim Qasimi highlights the unique feature of 'Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair' in providing a panoramic view of fiqh through legal maxims. It stresses that the book's real value emerges only when taught by a teacher who himself possesses the ability of istinbat (deduction) and who engages students in practical exercises. Mere lecturing is insufficient. For students with an inclination towards ifta (fatwa-giving), this book holds extraordinary importance.

Guided Path
1
Identify the unique feature of Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair
According to the taqriz, the book provides a comprehensive perspective linking fiqh issues through maxims, enabling deduction of future rulings.
2
Extract the teacher's required qualification
The teacher must himself possess the skill of istinbat (deduction) and engage students in practical application.
3
Determine the consequence of lacking this qualification
Without it, the book becomes an ordinary text and its teaching holds no importance.
4
Connect to the madrasa context
Madrasas entrust its teaching to specially qualified teachers; administrators should empower such teachers.
5
Relate to the student of ifta
For students inclined towards ifta, the book is exceptionally important and must be taught with practical istinbat exercises.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
تقريظ :
خطیب الاسلام حضرت مولانا محمد سالم صاحب مدظلہ العالی صدر باشم ودار العلوم وقف و سینئر نائب صدر مسلم پر نساء بورد
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
الاشباه والنظائر - فقہی متون میں دوری نقطہ نظر سے ایسی خصوصیت پر مشتمل ہے کہ مسائل مستقبل کے عمل استناد کر اس خصوصیت کی درساتہ جمانی [؟] بھی کرتا ہواور ساتھ ہی امثلہ پر انطباق سے اس کی توضیح بھی کی جارہی ہو۔ کی جانب ایماں کی وجہ سے طریقہ استنباط کی صلاحیت اس کتاب سے پیدا ہو سکتی ہے، بشرطیکہ معلم بذات خود اس صلاحیت کا حامل ہو اس لحاظ سے اس کتاب کی تدریس بڑی اہمیت کی حامل بن جاتی ہے اس کی تدریس میں اس خصوصیت کا شمول بھی
در حقیقت اس کا قرار واقعی حق تدریس ادا کر سکتا ہے اس کے بغیر اس کتاب کی تدریس کسی اہمیت کی حامل نہیں ہوتی۔ اس لیے مدارس میں اس کی تدریس عموماً اس خاص صلاحیت کے حامل اساتذہ سے متعلق کی جاتی ہے اس کے بغیر یہ کتاب ایک عام متن منتہا سے زیادہ کسی اہمیت کی حامل نہیں رہتی پھر افتاء سے ذوقاً مناسبت رکھنے والے طلبہ کے لیے یہ کتاب دیگر کتب فقہیہ کے متقابل غیر معمولی اہمیت کی حامل بن جاتی ہے۔ اس کتاب کی تدریس میں طلبہ کو تمرینا استنباط مسائل کی تفاصیل پر بھی وقتا فوقتا لگایا جانا ضروری ہوتا ہے اس لیے طالب علم میں یہ امتیاز محض درس تقریر پیدا نہیں کر سکتی گویا اس کے بغیر اس کی تدریس کسی رفع مقام کی حامل نہیں بنتی۔ اس لیے بہتر یہ ہوگا کہ اس کی تدریس سے پیشتر اساتذہ اس کی فقہی اور فنی امتیازات سے قرار واقعی واقفیت
حاصل کریں۔ اور اس پر بصیرت پیدا ہونے کے بعد اس کی تدریس کا قرار واقعی حق ادا کیا جا سکتا ہے۔ اس لیے ارباب مدارس با ذوق اساتذہ کو اس کتاب کی تدریس کا حق واقعی ادا کرنے کے قابل بنا کر اس کی تدریس شروع کرائیں، جس سے یقین ہے کہ طلبہ صحیح طور پر اس سے مستفید ہو سکیں گے۔ عزیزم مولوی محمد معصوم قاسمی ناظم جامعہ اسلامیہ مدرسہ المؤمنین منگلور ضلع ہریدوار اتراکھنڈ نے ” شرح النظائر کے نام سے الاشباہ والنظائر " کی ایک شرح تالیف کی ہے جس میں حل عبارت پر خصوصی توجہ دی گئی ہے، ترجمہ میں سہل زبان استعمال کی گئی ہے اور تشریح میں آسان اسلوب اختیار کیا گیا ہے۔
دعا ہے کہ اللہ رب العزت اس شرح کو شان قبولیت سے سرفراز کرے ۔ (آمین
Endorsement:
Khatib al-Islam Hazrat Maulana Muhammad Salim Sahib, may his shadow be extended, Chairman of Darul Uloom Waqf and Senior Vice President of Muslim Prens Board
In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.
Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair - among fiqh texts, from a comprehensive perspective, has such a feature that issues of the future, relying on action, this feature of teaching and training [؟] also does, and at the same time, through application of examples, its explanation is also being done. Because of the inclination towards it, the ability of the method of deduction can be developed from this book, provided that the teacher himself possesses this ability. In this regard, the teaching of this book becomes very important. Including this feature in its teaching
in reality can fulfill its proper right of teaching; without it, the teaching of this book holds no importance. Therefore, in madrasas, its teaching is generally entrusted to teachers who possess this special ability. Without it, this book remains nothing more than an ordinary text. Then for students who have a natural inclination towards ifta, this book becomes of extraordinary importance compared to other fiqh books. In teaching this book, it is necessary to engage students in the practice of deduction of issues in detail from time to time, because this distinction cannot be produced in a student by mere lecture. So without it, its teaching cannot achieve any high status. Therefore, it is better that before teaching it, teachers gain a proper acquaintance with its fiqh and technical distinctions.
And after gaining insight into it, the proper right of its teaching can be fulfilled. Therefore, the administrators of madrasas should empower passionate teachers to fulfill the real right of teaching this book and start its teaching, from which it is certain that students will benefit from it correctly. My dear son, Maulvi Muhammad Masum Qasimi, principal of Jamia Islamiya Madrasa al-Mu'minin, Mangalur, district Haridwar, Uttarakhand, has authored a commentary of Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair named Sharh al-Nazair, in which special attention has been given to the explanation of phrases, simple language has been used in translation, and an easy style has been adopted in commentary.
Prayer that Allah, Lord of Might, may honor this commentary with acceptance. (Ameen)
Source pages p. 4

Commentary
This is a taqriz (endorsement) by Muhammad Salim Qasimi for the commentary 'Sharh al-Nazair' on 'Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair'. The passage discusses the unique feature of the book in providing a panoramic view of fiqh issues by linking them through legal maxims. It emphasizes that effective teaching of this book requires a teacher who himself possesses the skill of istinbat (deduction of rulings) and who engages students in practical exercises. Mere lecturing is insufficient. The endorsement also praises the author's commentary for its clear language and style.

Key Terms
تقريظ (taqriz): An endorsement or commendation, often written by a senior scholar to introduce a book.
استنباط (istinbat): Deduction or derivation of legal rulings from primary sources or legal maxims.
الاشباه والنظائر (Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair): A classical Hanafi work by Ibn Nujaym compiling legal maxims (qawaid) and similar cases.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What does the taqriz identify as essential for the teaching of Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair to be effective?
A) The teacher must be a master of Arabic grammar.
B) The teacher must possess the skill of istinbat and engage students in practical deduction exercises.
C) The teacher should only use the original text without commentary.
D) Students must memorize all maxims before any explanation.

Key Takeaway
Effective teaching of Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair requires teachers skilled in istinbat and students engaged in practical deduction, not mere memorization.

Introduction and Front Matter

The Pedagogical Value of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair in Hanafi Ifta Training
Endorsement emphasizing the teaching methodology and importance of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain why al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair is essential for developing istinbat skills in ifta training and identify the conditions for its effective teaching.

Core Idea
Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair trains the mufti in istinbat — not just memorising maxims.

This endorsement by Muhammad Salim Qasimi highlights the unique role of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair in Hanafi legal education. Unlike a mere compendium of rulings, this book cultivates the skill of deriving new rulings by applying qawa'id to novel cases. The passage stresses that its true value is unlocked only when the teacher himself masters istinbat and when students engage in regular exercises.

Guided Path
1
Identify the distinctive characteristic of the book
From the text, the book is distinguished by its reliance on applying future rulings through examples, building the skill of istinbat.
This is not just a collection of maxims; it is a training tool.
2
State the teacher's prerequisite
The teacher must himself possess the ability of istinbat; otherwise, the book loses its importance.
The author says the teacher 'bakhud is salahiyyat ka hamil ho'.
3
Explain the benefit for ifta students
For students inclined toward fatwa issuance, this book becomes extraordinarily important compared to other fiqh texts.
It builds the practical skill of applying maxims to real cases.
4
Highlight the role of practical exercises
Regular practice in deriving rulings is necessary; lecture alone cannot produce the required distinction in a student.
The text says 'tamrinan istinbat masail ki tafsilaat par bhi waqtan faqtan lagaya jana zaroori hota hai'.

Source Text

تقريظ :
خطیب الاسلام حضرت مولانا محمد سالم صاحب مدظلہ العالی صدر باشم ودار العلوم وقف و سینئر نائب صدر مسلم پر نساء بورد
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
الاشباه والنظائر - فقہی متون میں دوری نقطہ نظر سے ایسی خصوصیت پر مشتمل ہے کہ مسائل مستقبل کے عمل استناد کر اس خصوصیت کی درساتہ [؟] جمانی بھی کرتا ہواور ساتھ ہی امثلہ پر انطباق سے اس کی توضیح بھی کی جارہی ہو۔ کی جانب ایماں کی وجہ سے طریقہ استنباط کی صلاحیت اس کتاب سے پیدا ہو سکتی ہے، بشرطیکہ معلم بذات خود اس صلاحیت کا حامل ہو اس لحاظ سے اس کتاب کی تدریس بڑی اہمیت کی حامل بن جاتی ہے اس کی تدریس میں اس خصوصیت کا شمول بھی
در حقیقت اس کا قرار واقعی حق تدریس ادا کر سکتا ہے اس کے بغیر اس کتاب کی تدریس کسی اہمیت کی حامل نہیں ہوتی۔ اس لیے مدارس میں اس کی تدریس عموماً اس خاص صلاحیت کے حامل اساتذہ سے متعلق کی جاتی ہے اس کے بغیر یہ کتاب ایک عام متن منتہا سے زیادہ کسی اہمیت کی حامل نہیں رہتی پھر افتاء سے ذوقاً مناسبت رکھنے والے طلبہ کے لیے یہ کتاب دیگر کتب فقہیہ کے متقابل غیر معمولی اہمیت کی حامل بن جاتی ہے۔ اس کتاب کی تدریس میں طلبہ کو تمرینا استنباط مسائل کی تفاصیل پر بھی وقتا فوقتا لگایا جانا ضروری ہوتا ہے اس لیے طالب علم میں یہ امتیاز محض درس تقریر پیدا نہیں کر سکتی گویا اس کے بغیر اس کی تدریس کسی رفع مقام کی حامل نہیں بنتی۔ اس لیے بہتر یہ ہوگا کہ اس کی تدریس سے پیشتر اساتذہ اس کی فقہی اور فنی امتیازات سے قرار واقعی واقفیت
حاصل کریں۔ اور اس پر بصیرت پیدا ہونے کے بعد اس کی تدریس کا قرار واقعی حق ادا کیا جا سکتا ہے۔ اس لیے ارباب مدارس با ذوق اساتذہ کو اس کتاب کی تدریس کا حق واقعی ادا کرنے کے قابل بنا کر اس کی تدریس شرد یا کرا ئیں ، جس سے یقین ہے کہ طلبہ صحیح طور پر اس سے مستفید ہو سکیں گے۔ عزیزم مولوی محمد معصوم قاسمی ناظم جامعہ اسلامیہ مدرسہ المؤمنین منگلور ضلع ہریدوار اتراکھنڈ نے ” شرح النظائر کے نام سے الاشباہ والنظائر " کی ایک شرح تالیف کی ہے جس میں حل عبارت پر خصوصی توجہ دی گئی ہے، ترجمہ میں سہل زبان استعمال کی گئی ہے اور تشریح میں آسان اسلوب اختیار کیا گیا ہے۔
دعا ہے کہ اللہ رب العزت اس شرح کو شان قبولیت سے سرفراز کرے ۔ (آمین
محمد سالم قاسمی
Endorsement: Khatib al-Islam Hazrat Maulana Muhammad Salim Sahib, may his shadow be exalted, Chairman of Darul Uloom Waqf and Senior Vice President of Muslim Personal Law Board. In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful. Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair - among Fiqh texts, from a distant perspective, it is distinguished by such a characteristic that it relies on the application of future rulings, and this characteristic is also being established, and along with that, it is being clarified through application to examples. Due to the element of faith, the ability of the method of derivation can be developed from this book, provided that the teacher himself possesses this ability. In this respect, the teaching of this book becomes very important. Its teaching includes this characteristic. In reality, it can fulfill the rightful duty of teaching; without it, the teaching of this book does not hold any importance. Therefore, in madrasas, its teaching is generally entrusted to teachers who possess this special ability. Without this, this book is no more important than a common text. Then, for students who have a natural inclination towards issuing fatwas, this book becomes extraordinarily important compared to other Fiqh books. In teaching this book, it is necessary to regularly engage students in exercises of deriving rulings on details. For this reason, the distinction in a student cannot be produced merely by lecture; thus, without it, its teaching does not achieve any high status. Therefore, it would be better that before its teaching, teachers thoroughly acquaint themselves with its Fiqh and technical distinctions. And after gaining insight into it, the rightful duty of its teaching can be fulfilled. Therefore, madrasa authorities should enable enthusiastic teachers to fulfill the real right of teaching this book and then assign its teaching, so that students can benefit from it correctly. My dear Maulvi Muhammad Masum Qasimi, the supervisor of Jami'a Islamiyya Madrassa al-Mu'minin, Mangalur, Haridwar district, Uttarakhand, has authored a commentary on Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair named 'Sharh al-Nazair', in which special attention has been given to explanation of phrases, easy language has been used in translation, and a simple style has been adopted in explanation. Prayer that Allah, the Lord of Might, may honor this commentary with acceptance. (Ameen) Muhammad Salim Qasimi
Source pages p. 4

Commentary
This passage is a taqriz (endorsement) by Muhammad Salim Qasimi for a commentary on al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair titled Sharh al-Nazair. The endorsement highlights the unique pedagogical value of the original text, emphasizing that it is not a mere collection of maxims but a tool for developing the skill of istinbat (legal derivation) through the application of qawa'id (legal maxims) to specific cases. The author stresses that effective teaching requires a teacher who himself possesses this skill; otherwise, the book loses its significance. He also underscores the importance of practical exercises for students, especially those inclined toward ifta' (fatwa issuance). The endorsement concludes with praise for the commentator's work, noting its clear language and accessible style.

Key Terms
تدریس (tadris): Teaching methodology, especially the act of transmitting knowledge with pedagogical skill
استنباط (istinbat): The process of deriving legal rulings from primary sources through ijtihad

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the endorsement, what is essential for effectively teaching al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair?
A) A teacher who has a large collection of fatwas
B) A teacher who himself possesses the skill of istinbat
C) A teacher who focuses only on memorization of maxims
D) A teacher who uses advanced technology

Key Takeaway
The effectiveness of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair depends on a teacher skilled in istinbat and regular student practice in deriving rulings.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
8 min
The Genius of Hanafi Fiqh and the Necessity of Taqlid
Endorsement lauding Hanafi fiqh and defending taqlid.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the significance of Hanafi fiqh as an intellectual discipline and defend the necessity of taqlid of the four imams using the arguments from the text.

Core Idea
Hanafi fiqh is a divinely gifted intellectual science; without taqlid, one cannot correctly practice Islam.

This endorsement by Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri introduces the book Sharh al-Nazair by extolling the greatness of Hanafi fiqh and its founding imams. The passage highlights the unparalleled depth of fiqh, the genius of Imam Abu Hanifa and his students, and the indispensable role of taqlid for every Muslim. It also critiques those who reject madhhab adherence, arguing that understanding the Book and Sunnah without fiqh methodology is impossible.

Guided Path
1
Grasp the author's praise of fiqh as a unique intellectual achievement
Read how the author describes fiqh as a 'magnificent creative achievement' with no parallel in other religions. Note the metaphor of honeybees distilling purified honey from Quran and Hadith.
This sets the tone for the entire work as a product of profound scholarship.
2
Identify the key figures and their contributions
Imam Abu Hanifa is called the 'originator and father of Islamic fiqh'. His students Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani are praised for their genius: Abu Yusuf for his famous judgments, Muhammad for his written works like al-Mabsut.
These three form the core of the Hanafi school's authority (zahir al-riwayah).
3
Analyze the Christian scholar's anecdote
A Christian scholar saw Imam Muhammad's al-Mabsut and exclaimed: 'When the book of your little Muhammad has such scope, what must be the scope of the Great Muhammad's book (the Quran)?' This highlights that fiqh is a reflection of the Quran's depth.
The anecdote shows that even non-Muslims recognize the intellectual power of Hanafi fiqh.
4
Understand the critique of anti-taqlid
The author criticizes those who reject following the four imams, calling it 'blindness' and 'following desires'. He asserts that without taqlid, one cannot even correctly perform wudu according to the Sunnah.
This is a strong defense of madhhab adherence as a practical necessity.
5
Connect to the necessity of studying fiqh
The passage underscores that fiqh is not optional; it is the key to implementing Shariah. Works like al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair are essential tools for mastering Hanafi fiqh.
This lesson sets the stage for studying the qawaid (legal maxims) in the book.

کہ انسان حیرت میں رہ جاتا ہے صحیح معنی میں قرآن وحدیث کی وہ نصوص کہ جن کا ادنی تعلق بھی کسی حکم سے ہوتا ہے فقہاء عظام رحمہم اللہ نے شہد کی مکھی کے مانند عرق کشید کر کے مسائل فقہیہ کا عسل مصفی تیار کر روزگار شخصیت بھی نہیں کر سکتی اللہ تعالی نے انہیں ذہانت ، فراست کے ساتھ اپنے فن میں کتنی گہرائی و گیرائی اور عبقریت عطاء فرمائی تھی اس کا اندازہ وہی لوگ کر سکتے ہیں جو فقہ وفتاویٰ سے مناسبت رکھتے ہیں بالخصوص الامام الاعظم ابو حنیفہ جو فقہ اسلامی کے موجد اور فقہاء امت کے بابائے آدم ہیں۔ فقہی بصیرت متحیر العقول، ذہانت، مدحش اور قوت اجتہاد حیرت انگیز اور ضرب المثل اسلامی فقیہ کا یہ شجره طوبی جب برگ وبارلا یا تو چشم فلک نے قاضی ابو یوسف امام محمد ابن حسن شیبائی جیسی نابغہ روزگار ہستیوں کا مشاہدہ کیا قاضی ابو یوسف کے فیصلے شہرہ آفاق تو امام محمد کی تصنیفی خدمات مشہور عالم کسی مسیحی اسکالر نے امام محمد کی معرکۃ الآراء کتاب مبسوط کو جب ایک مسیحی اسکالر نے دیکھا تو حیرت سے آنکھیں پھٹی کی پھٹی رہ گئیں اور ایک عجیب جملہ زبان سے نکلا جس کا مفہوم یہ تھا کہ " تمہارے چھوٹے محمد کی کتاب کا جب یہ عالم ہے کے طول و عرض
Endorsement: Hazrat Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, may his shadow be exalted, teacher of Hadith at Darul Uloom Waqf Deoband. Islamic Fiqh is that magnificent creative achievement of Islamic scholars, the like of which is not found in any other religion besides Islam. Discussion and research on every subject of the religion and every aspect of Shariah with such subtlety that a person remains amazed. In the true sense, the texts of Quran and Hadith that have even the slightest connection to any ruling—the great jurists, may Allah have mercy on them, have distilled like a honeybee and prepared the purified honey of Fiqh issues, which will continue to be healing, satisfying, and life-giving for the Muslim Ummah until the Day of Judgment. The common person cannot match the profound insight and delicate vision of the great jurists, nay, even the proud personalities of other sciences and arts cannot compete. The depth, breadth, and genius that Allah granted them in their field—only those who are connected to Fiqh and fatwas can appreciate it, especially Imam al-A'zam Abu Hanifa, who is the originator of Islamic Fiqh and the father of the jurists of the Ummah. His Fiqh insight bewilders minds, his intelligence is astonishing, and his power of ijtihad is amazing and proverbial. When this blessed tree of Islamic Fiqh bore fruit, the eye of fate witnessed geniuses like Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad ibn Hasan al-Shaybani. Qadi Abu Yusuf's judgments are world-famous, and Imam Muhammad's written works are renowned in the world. A Christian scholar, when he saw Imam Muhammad's monumental work al-Mabsut, was astonished and exclaimed: 'When the book of your little Muhammad has such a scope, then what must be the scope of the book of the Great Muhammad (peace be upon him) (the Quran)?' It is the misfortune or blindness of a section of the Ummat that this brilliant achievement of the great jurists holds no meaning in their eyes. This group considers following their own desires as superior to following the four Imams, and even bestow titles like misguidance and error upon following the Imams, while they know that understanding the rulings and meanings of the Book and Sunnah without following one of the four Imams is no easy task. The truth is that without Fiqh, it is impossible for a person to even perform wudu according to the Sunnah. This group, in recent years, has spread like monsoon insects across the length and breadth of the country.
Source pages p. 5

Commentary
This is a taqriz (endorsement) by Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, praising the book Sharh al-Nazair and highlighting the greatness of Hanafi fiqh. The passage extols the intellectual achievement of Islamic jurisprudence, particularly the Hanafi school, emphasizing the unparalleled depth and precision of its scholars. The author recounts the famous story of a Christian scholar who was awed by Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani's al-Mabsut, leading him to exclaim about the Quran's grandeur. The taqriz also criticizes those who reject taqlid (following a madhhab), arguing that without fiqh, one cannot even perform wudu correctly. This serves to underscore the necessity of the Hanafi method and the value of studying works like al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair.

Key Terms
تقلید (taqlid): Following a qualified Imam (mujtahid) in legal rulings, considered obligatory for non-mujtahids
فقہ (fiqh): Islamic jurisprudence, the science of deriving practical rulings from detailed evidence

Key Terms from Source Passage

Key Takeaway
Hanafi fiqh is an indispensable intellectual heritage; taqlid of the four imams is necessary for correct Islamic practice.

Introduction and Front Matter
intermediate
8 min
Fiqh: The Crown of Islamic Learning and the Necessity of Taqlid
Defense of taqlid and praise of fiqh

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain why the Hanafi tradition considers taqlid of the four Imams necessary for correct practice, and cite the argument from the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab supporting it.

Core Idea
Without following a mujtahid imam, even wudu cannot be performed correctly — taqlid is a practical necessity, not a luxury.

The taqriz penned by Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri opens with a soaring praise of Islamic jurisprudence, comparing the jurists' work to honeybees extracting pure honey. He then turns to a vigorous defense of taqlid, addressing those who claim to follow only Quran and Sunnah directly. This lesson unpacks his argument and the crucial quotation from the Hanbali reform movement that even they require laymen to follow one of the four Imams.

Guided Path
1
Identify the praise of fiqh
The author extols fiqh as a unique achievement of Islamic scholarship. Note the honeybee analogy: jurists extract rulings like honey from the Quran and Sunnah. This establishes the high status of fiqh.
This sets the stage for defending the scholars who developed the madhhabs.
2
Highlight the central role of Imam Abu Hanifa
Imam Abu Hanifa is called the originator of Islamic fiqh and the father of the jurists. His students Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad are praised. This shows the authoritative chain of the Hanafi school.
The anecdote about the Christian scholar amazed by al-Mabsut underscores the depth of Hanafi scholarship.
3
Analyze the criticism of anti-taqlid groups
The author laments a group that considers following the four Imams as misguidance and follows its own desires. He argues that without taqlid, one cannot even perform wudu correctly.
This is the core of the defense: taqlid is practically essential for proper Islamic practice.
4
Examine the quote from Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab's son
The son states that they follow Imam Ahmad in subsidiary matters and do not deny taqlid of the four Imams; they even compel others to follow one of them. This is a powerful rebuttal to those who claim the reformers rejected taqlid.
The quote is from al-Durar al-Saniyya, showing that even the Najdi movement upheld taqlid of the four.
5
Conclude the author's purpose
The taqriz aims to affirm that taqlid is not optional but a necessity for Muslims not qualified for ijtihad. The author uses both rational argument and textual evidence (the quote) to support his position.
This lesson equips the student with a key argument in the debate about taqlid.

الامام الاعظم ابو حنیفہ جو فقہ اسلامی کے موجد اور فقہاء امت کے بابائے آدم ہیں۔ فقہی بصیرت متحیر العقول، ذہانت، مدحش اور قوت اجتہاد حیرت انگیز اور ضرب المثل اسلامی فقیہ کا یہ شجره طوبی جب برگ وبارلا یا تو چشم فلک نے قاضی ابو یوسف امام محمد ابن حسن شیبائی جیسی نابغہ روزگار ہستیوں کا مشاہدہ کیا قاضی ابو یوسف کے فیصلے شہرہ آفاق تو امام محمد کی تصنیفی خدمات مشہور عالم کسی مسیحی اسکالر نے امام محمد کی معرکۃ الآراء کتاب مبسوط کو جب ایک مسیحی اسکالر نے دیکھا تو حیرت سے آنکھیں پھٹی کی پھٹی رہ گئیں اور ایک عجیب جملہ زبان سے نکلا جس کا مفہوم یہ تھا کہ " تمہارے چھوٹے محمد کی کتاب کا جب یہ عالم ہے تو بڑے محمد (صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم ) کی کتاب (قرآن کریم کا عالم کیا ہوگا ؟ امت کے ایک طبقہ کی حرماں نصیبی کہئے یا کور دماغی اس کی نظر میں فقہاء کرام کا یہ عبقری کا رنامہ کوئی معنی ہی نہیں رکھتا، یہ طبقہ ہوائے نفس کی تقلید کو ائمہ اربعہ کی تقلید سے نہ صرف افضل تصور کرتا ہے بلکہ تقلید ائمہ کو ضلال اور گمراہی جیسے القاب سے نوازتا ہے حالانکہ انہیں معلوم ہے کہ ائمہ اربعہ میں سے کسی ایک کی تقلید کئے بغیر کتاب وسنت کے احکام اور مفاہیم کو سمجھنا کوئی آسان کام نہیں اور سچ یہ ہے کہ فقہ کے بغیر کسی شخص کے لئے یہ مکن ہی نہیں کہ وہ سنت کے مطابق وضوء ہی کر لے یہ طبقہ ادھر چند سالوں سے برساتی کیڑوں کی طرح ملک کے طول و عرض میں پھیل رہا ہے ائمہ کرام پر ایسی ایسی افتراء پردازیاں کہ شیطان بھی پناہ مانگے ۔ ہندوستان کے بعض خطوں میں سادہ لوح مسلمان اس مطلق العنان اور ہوا پرست جماعت کے ہاتھوں اپنے دین کے بارے میں جس تحمہ اور کشمکش میں مبتلا ہیں اس کا بدترین نتیجہ بعض اوقات دین سے انحراف کی شکل میں سامنے آتا ہے کٹ حجتی اور ضد کا یہ عالم ہے کہ ان زخموں پر فکری وحدت کا مرہم رکھنے کی ضرورت ہے نہ کہ اساطین امت پر تنقیص کر کے نمک چھر کنے کی۔ ذرا بھی یہ احساس نہیں ہوتا کہ اس وقت امت مسلمہ جس اندرونی و بیرونی انتشار اور اختلاف کے زخموں سے چور ہے علمی مسکنت اور کور باطنی کہیں پیچھے چھوڑے تو محمد بن عبد الوہاب کے بیٹے کی وضاحت اس طبقہ کے لئے تھی چشم کشا ہے "ونحن أيضاً في الفروع على مذهب الامام احمد ابن حنبل ولا ننكر على من قلد احداً من الأئمة الأربعة دون غيرهم لعدم ضبط مذاهب الغير الرافضة الزيدية والامامية ونحوهم ولانجير هم على الفاسدة بل نجبر هم على تقليد احد الائمة الأربعة الدر السنية : ج/ ١ /ص/٣٢٧ ملاحظہ فرمائیے تا خلف اخلاف کو فاضل اسلاف نے کیسا آئینہ دکھایا " فهل من مدكر" فقہ اسلامی پر لکھی گئی کتابوں کا زیادہ تر ذخیرہ تو براہ راست تشریح احکام سے تعلق رکھتا ہے، ان میں جو زیادہ جامع اور معیاری ذخیرہ ہے وہ صدیوں سے مدارس اسلامیہ کے نصاب میں شامل ہے ۔ ان میں کچھ کتا میں خالص فقہی اصول و قواعد سے تعلق رکھتی ہیں جن میں چند کتب نہایت مشہور اور متداول ہیں۔ رسالہ الکری لابی محسن بی الحسین الکرخی (وفات: ۳۴۰ھ) اس پر علامہ نجم الدین ابو حفص عمر بن احمد النسلی (وفات: ۵۳۷ھ) نے امثلہ نگار اور شواہد کا اضافہ کیا ہے جو " تاسیس انظر" کے ساتھ مطبوع ہے۔ تاسیس انظر لابن زید عبید الله بن عمر بن عیسی الا بوسی (وفات: ۴۳۰ ھ ) مجامع الحقائق لأبي سعيد حمد المال (وفات: ۱۱۷۶ھ ) منافع الدقائق شرح مجامع الحقائق مصطفیٰ بن محمد الکوزی انحصاری (وفات: ۱۳۱۵ھ ) الفرائد الحمیہ نے القواعد والفرائد الفقیه محمود حمزه لختی دمشق (وفات: ۱۳۰۵) نجیم (وفات: ۹۸۰ھ) ہے۔ یہ کتاب قواعد فقہیہ تطبیقیہ میں سے ہے، جس میں قواعد فقہیہ کی تطبیق مسائل اور فروع پر اتنے مبسوط اور مفصل میں کی گئی ہے کہ ان قواعد کی روشنی میں ایک فقیہ ہر زمانہ اور ہر جگہ نوازل اور وقائع کے احکام کا استنباط کر سکتا ہے۔ یہ کتاب اپنے موضوع پر زبر دست اہمیت کی حامل ہے اس لیے اس کو افتاء کے طلباء کو پڑھایا جاتا ہے تا کہ ان کے اندر استنباط کتاب کی غیر معمولی اہمیت کے پیش نظر فاضل گرامی جناب مولانا مفتی محمد معصوم قاسمی ناظم مدرسة المومنین ان سب میں بے نظیر اور نصاب درس میں شامل الاشباہ والنظائر للامام زین الدین بن ابیر ام محمد الشهر بان احکام کی صلاحیت پیدا ہو۔
Taqriz: by Hadrat Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, may his shadow lengthen, teacher of Hadith at Darul Uloom Waqf Deoband. Islamic jurisprudence is that magnificent creative achievement of the scholars of Islam, the example of which is not found in any other religion besides Islam. On every subject of religion and every aspect of Sharia, there is such detailed discussion, research, and analysis that one remains amazed. In the true sense, from the texts of the Quran and Hadith, even the slightest connection of which is with any ruling, the great jurists (may Allah have mercy on them) extracted like the honeybee and prepared the refined honey of juristic issues, which will remain healing, refreshing, and life-giving for the Muslim Ummah until the Day of Judgment. The deep insight and profound vision of the great jurists cannot be matched by ordinary humans, let alone by the proud personalities of other sciences and arts. Allah had granted them such intelligence, perspicacity, depth, breadth, and genius in their field that only those who are associated with fiqh and fatwa can estimate it, especially Imam al-A'zam Abu Hanifa, who is the originator of Islamic fiqh and the father of the jurists of the Ummah. His juristic insight is mind-boggling, his intelligence is astounding, and his power of ijtihad is amazing and proverbial. When this tree of Tuba of the Islamic jurist bore fruit, the eye of the sky witnessed geniuses like Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad ibn Hasan al-Shaybani. The verdicts of Qadi Abu Yusuf are world-famous, while the literary works of Imam Muhammad are world-renowned. A Christian scholar, when he saw Imam Muhammad's ground-breaking book al-Mabsut, his eyes remained wide with astonishment, and a strange sentence came from his tongue, the meaning of which was: 'If this is the state of your small Muhammad's book, then what would be the state of the book of the Great Muhammad (peace be upon him), the Holy Quran?' It is either the misfortune of a section of the Ummah or their mental blindness that in their view this genius achievement of the great jurists has no meaning. This section considers following one's own desires superior to following the four Imams, and even labels following the Imams as misguidance and error, although they know that without following one of the four Imams, understanding the commands and concepts of the Book and Sunnah is not an easy task. The truth is that without fiqh, it is not possible for a person to even perform wudu according to the Sunnah. This group has been spreading like monsoon insects across the length and breadth of the country for the past few years. They make such slanderous allegations against the great Imams that even Satan would seek refuge. In some regions of India, simple Muslims are engulfed in such turmoil and conflict regarding their religion at the hands of this absolute and whimsical group that the worst result sometimes appears in the form of deviation from religion. This is a state of obstinacy and stubbornness that there is a need to apply the balm of intellectual unity on these wounds, not to sprinkle salt by condemning the pillars of the Ummah. There is no realization at all that the Muslim Ummah is now afflicted with internal and external dissension and conflict. If academic humility and inner blindness could be left behind, then the clarification of the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab would be eye-opening for this group: 'And we too are in subsidiary matters upon the madhhab of Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal, and we do not deny one who follows any one of the four Imams to the exclusion of others, because the madhhabs of others (like the Rafidah, Zaydis, Imamis, and the like) are not preserved, and we do not allow them upon the corrupt, rather we compel them to follow one of the four Imams.' (al-Durar al-Saniyya, vol. 1, p. 327) Take note of how the virtuous predecessors showed a mirror to the successors. 'Is there then anyone who will take heed?' Most of the writings on Islamic jurisprudence are directly related to the explanation of rulings. Among them, the more comprehensive and standard works have been included in the curriculum of Islamic seminaries for centuries. Among these, some books are related purely to juristic principles and rules, of which a few are very famous and widely circulated. Risalah al-Karkhi by Abu Muhsin al-Husayn al-Karkhi (d. 340 AH); Allama Najm al-Din Abu Hafs Umar ibn Ahmad al-Nasafi (d. 537 AH) added examples and evidences to it, which is printed with Ta'sis al-Nazar. Ta'sis al-Nazar by Ubayd Allah ibn Umar ibn Isa al-Abusi (d. 430 AH). Majami' al-Haqa'iq by Abu Sa'id [illegible] (d. 1176 AH). Manafi' al-Daqa'iq, a commentary on Majami' al-Haqa'iq by Mustafa ibn Muhammad al-Kawzi al-Ansari (d. 1315 AH). Al-Fara'id al-Hamiyya on al-Qawa'id wa al-Fara'id al-Fiqhiyya by Mahmud Hamza al-Khatib al-Dimashqi (d. 1305 AH). [Najm?] (d. 980 AH). This book is among the applied juristic rules, in which the application of juristic rules to issues and branches has been done so extensively and in detail that a jurist can deduce the rulings of new occurrences and events in every time and place in the light of these rules. This book is of paramount importance on its subject, therefore it is taught to students of ifta' so that they may develop the ability to deduce rulings. Due to the extraordinary importance of the book, the honorable scholar, Maulana Mufti Muhammad Mas'um Qasmi, the principal of Madrasatul Momineen, and it is unparalleled and included in the curriculum: al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Imam Zayn al-Din ibn [Abi?] Muhammad al-Shahrazuri.
Source pages p. 5

Commentary
This passage is a taqriz (introductory eulogy) written by Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, a Hadith teacher at Darul Uloom Waqf Deoband, praising the science of fiqh and defending the necessity of taqlid (following the four Imams). The author begins by extolling Islamic fiqh as a unique intellectual achievement unparalleled in any other religion. He highlights the meticulousness of the great jurists in extracting rulings from the Quran and Hadith, comparing them to bees producing pure honey. He then specifically praises Imam Abu Hanifa as the originator of Islamic fiqh and mentions his illustrious students, Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani. An anecdote is related about a Christian scholar amazed by the depth of Imam Muhammad's 'al-Mabsut'. The author then criticizes a group (apparently Ghayr Muqallids or similar) who oppose taqlid of the four Imams and follow their own desires. He argues that without following one of the four Imams, even performing wudu correctly is impossible. To support his argument, he quotes from the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab, who stated that they follow Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal in subsidiary matters and compel Muslims to follow one of the four Imams, rejecting the madhhabs of the Rafidah, Zaydis, etc. The taqriz then transitions to discussing important works on usul al-fiqh and qawaid fiqhiyya (legal maxims), listing several key texts: Risalah al-Karkhi, Ta'sis al-Nazar, Majami' al-Haqa'iq, Manafi' al-Daqa'iq, al-Fara'id al-Hamiyya, and finally the book itself, al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Imam Zayn al-Din al-Shahrazuri. The author emphasizes the importance of these books for students of ifta' to develop the ability to deduce rulings for new situations.

Key Terms
فقہ اسلامی (fiqh islami): Islamic jurisprudence, the science of extracting legal rulings from the Quran, Sunnah, Ijma, and Qiyas.
تقلید (taqlid): Following one of the four recognized Imams in subsidiary matters of fiqh.
ائمہ اربعہ (a'imma arba'a): The four founders of the Sunni madhhabs: Abu Hanifa, Maliki, Shafi'i, and Ahmad ibn Hanbal.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the taqriz, what is the consequence of rejecting taqlid of the four Imams?
A) One becomes a kafir.
B) One cannot even perform wudu correctly according to Sunnah.
C) One's prayers are invalid.
D) One must follow a fifth madhhab.

Key Takeaway
Taqlid of one of the four Imams is not optional but a practical necessity for correct Islamic practice, as even basic acts like wudu require juristic interpretation.

Introduction and Front Matter
intermediate
6 min
The Foundational Works of Hanafi Qawaid Fiqhiyya for Ifta'
List of foundational qawaid works for ifta' training

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to list the major classical works on Hanafi qawaid fiqhiyya and explain their role in training a mufti to derive rulings for new cases.

Core Idea
A mufti must master the science of qawaid to apply legal maxims to new situations — the classical texts listed are the essential toolkit.

After defending taqlid, the taqriz transitions to the study of legal maxims (qawaid fiqhiyya). It lists several foundational texts that have been part of the madrasa curriculum for centuries. This lesson guides you through these works, explaining their significance for ifta' training and how they enable a jurist to deduce rulings for unprecedented events (nawazil).

Guided Path
1
Identify the transition in the passage
After the defense of taqlid, the author shifts to discussing the written corpus of fiqh, specifically works on usul and qawaid. Note the phrase 'بعض کتب خالص فقہی اصول و قواعد سے تعلق رکھتی ہیں' (some books are related purely to juristic principles and rules).
This signals that the following list is of specialized qawaid works.
2
List each work mentioned with its author
Go through the passage and extract each book title and its author. The list includes: Risalah al-Karkhi (al-Karkhi), Ta'sis al-Nazar (al-Abusi), Majami' al-Haqa'iq (author unclear), Manafi' al-Daqa'iq (al-Kawzi al-Ansari), al-Fara'id al-Hamiyya (Mahmud Hamza), and finally al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir (al-Shahrazuri).
Some names may be corrupted due to OCR; refer to the commentary for corrections.
3
Understand the purpose of these works
The author states that these books are taught to students of ifta' to develop the ability to deduce rulings (istinbat) for new events. They contain the application of qawaid to numerous branches (furu') so that a jurist can face any new situation.
This shows the practical, applied nature of the study of qawaid.
4
Focus on the book al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir
The taqriz ends by praising al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir as unparalleled and included in the curriculum. This book is the main subject of the text you are studying. Recognize its centrality.
This sets the stage for your detailed study of this work in subsequent lessons.

فقہ اسلامی علماء اسلام کا وہ عظیم الشان تخلیقی کارنامہ ہے کہ جس کی مثال اسلام کے علاوہ کسی دوسرے مذھب میں نہیں ملتی دین کے ہر موضوع اور شریعت کے ہر پہلو پر اتنی باریکی سے بحث و گفتگو اور تحقیق و تجزیہ وسنت کے احکام اور مفاہیم کو سمجھنا کوئی آسان کام نہیں اور سچ یہ ہے کہ فقہ کے بغیر کسی شخص کے لئے یہ مکن ہی نہیں کہ وہ سنت کے مطابق وضوء ہی کر لے یہ طبقہ ادھر چند سالوں سے برساتی کیڑوں کی طرح ملک کے طول و عرض میں پھیل رہا ہے ائمہ کرام پر ایسی ایسی افتراء پردازیاں کہ شیطان بھی پناہ مانگے ۔ ہندوستان کے بعض خطوں میں سادہ لوح مسلمان اس مطلق العنان اور ہوا پرست جماعت کے ہاتھوں اپنے دین کے بارے میں جس تحمہ اور کشمکش میں مبتلا ہیں اس کا بدترین نتیجہ بعض اوقات دین سے انحراف کی شکل میں سامنے آتا ہے کٹ حجتی اور ضد کا یہ عالم ہے کہ ان زخموں پر فکری وحدت کا مرہم رکھنے کی ضرورت ہے نہ کہ اساطین امت پر تنقیص کر کے نمک چھر کنے کی۔ ذرا بھی یہ احساس نہیں ہوتا کہ اس وقت امت مسلمہ جس اندرونی و بیرونی انتشار اور اختلاف کے زخموں سے چور ہے علمی مسکنت اور کور باطنی کہیں پیچھے چھوڑے تو محمد بن عبد الوہاب کے بیٹے کی وضاحت اس طبقہ کے لئے تھی چشم کشا ہے "ونحن أيضاً في الفروع على مذهب الامام احمد ابن حنبل ولا ننكر على من قلد احداً من الأئمة الأربعة دون غيرهم لعدم ضبط مذاهب الغير الرافضة الزيدية والامامية ونحوهم ولانجير هم على الفاسدة بل نجبر هم على تقليد احد الائمة الأربعة الدر السنية : ج/ ١ /ص/٣٢٧ ملاحظہ فرمائیے تا خلف اخلاف کو فاضل اسلاف نے کیسا آئینہ دکھایا " فهل من مدكر" فقہ اسلامی پر لکھی گئی کتابوں کا زیادہ تر ذخیرہ تو براہ راست تشریح احکام سے تعلق رکھتا ہے، ان میں جو زیادہ جامع اور معیاری ذخیرہ ہے وہ صدیوں سے مدارس اسلامیہ کے نصاب میں شامل ہے ۔ ان میں کچھ کتا میں خالص فقہی اصول و قواعد سے تعلق رکھتی ہیں جن میں چند کتب نہایت مشہور اور متداول ہیں۔ رسالہ الکری لابی محسن بی الحسین الکرخی (وفات: ۳۴۰ھ) اس پر علامہ نجم الدین ابو حفص عمر بن احمد النسلی (وفات: ۵۳۷ھ) نے امثلہ نگار اور شواہد کا اضافہ کیا ہے جو " تاسیس انظر" کے ساتھ مطبوع ہے۔ تاسیس انظر لابن زید عبید الله بن عمر بن عیسی الا بوسی (وفات: ۴۳۰ ھ ) مجامع الحقائق لأبي سعيد حمد المال (وفات: ۱۱۷۶ھ ) منافع الدقائق شرح مجامع الحقائق مصطفیٰ بن محمد الکوزی انحصاری (وفات: ۱۳۱۵ھ ) الفرائد الحمیہ نے القواعد والفرائد الفقیه محمود حمزه لختی دمشق (وفات: ۱۳۰۵) نجیم (وفات: ۹۸۰ھ) ہے۔ یہ کتاب قواعد فقہیہ تطبیقیہ میں سے ہے، جس میں قواعد فقہیہ کی تطبیق مسائل اور فروع پر اتنے مبسوط اور مفصل میں کی گئی ہے کہ ان قواعد کی روشنی میں ایک فقیہ ہر زمانہ اور ہر جگہ نوازل اور وقائع کے احکام کا استنباط کر سکتا ہے۔ یہ کتاب اپنے موضوع پر زبر دست اہمیت کی حامل ہے اس لیے اس کو افتاء کے طلباء کو پڑھایا جاتا ہے تا کہ ان کے اندر استنباط کتاب کی غیر معمولی اہمیت کے پیش نظر فاضل گرامی جناب مولانا مفتی محمد معصوم قاسمی ناظم مدرسة المومنین ان سب میں بے نظیر اور نصاب درس میں شامل الاشباہ والنظائر للامام زین الدین بن ابیر ام محمد الشهر بان احکام کی صلاحیت پیدا ہو۔
Taqriz: by Hadrat Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, may his shadow lengthen, teacher of Hadith at Darul Uloom Waqf Deoband. Islamic jurisprudence is that magnificent creative achievement of the scholars of Islam, the example of which is not found in any other religion besides Islam. On every subject of religion and every aspect of Sharia, there is such detailed discussion, research, and analysis that one remains amazed. In the true sense, from the texts of the Quran and Hadith, even the slightest connection of which is with any ruling, the great jurists (may Allah have mercy on them) extracted like the honeybee and prepared the refined honey of juristic issues, which will remain healing, refreshing, and life-giving for the Muslim Ummah until the Day of Judgment. The deep insight and profound vision of the great jurists cannot be matched by ordinary humans, let alone by the proud personalities of other sciences and arts. Allah had granted them such intelligence, perspicacity, depth, breadth, and genius in their field that only those who are associated with fiqh and fatwa can estimate it, especially Imam al-A'zam Abu Hanifa, who is the originator of Islamic fiqh and the father of the jurists of the Ummah. His juristic insight is mind-boggling, his intelligence is astounding, and his power of ijtihad is amazing and proverbial. When this tree of Tuba of the Islamic jurist bore fruit, the eye of the sky witnessed geniuses like Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad ibn Hasan al-Shaybani. The verdicts of Qadi Abu Yusuf are world-famous, while the literary works of Imam Muhammad are world-renowned. A Christian scholar, when he saw Imam Muhammad's ground-breaking book al-Mabsut, his eyes remained wide with astonishment, and a strange sentence came from his tongue, the meaning of which was: 'If this is the state of your small Muhammad's book, then what would be the state of the book of the Great Muhammad (peace be upon him), the Holy Quran?' It is either the misfortune of a section of the Ummah or their mental blindness that in their view this genius achievement of the great jurists has no meaning. This section considers following one's own desires superior to following the four Imams, and even labels following the Imams as misguidance and error, although they know that without following one of the four Imams, understanding the commands and concepts of the Book and Sunnah is not an easy task. The truth is that without fiqh, it is not possible for a person to even perform wudu according to the Sunnah. This group has been spreading like monsoon insects across the length and breadth of the country for the past few years. They make such slanderous allegations against the great Imams that even Satan would seek refuge. In some regions of India, simple Muslims are engulfed in such turmoil and conflict regarding their religion at the hands of this absolute and whimsical group that the worst result sometimes appears in the form of deviation from religion. This is a state of obstinacy and stubbornness that there is a need to apply the balm of intellectual unity on these wounds, not to sprinkle salt by condemning the pillars of the Ummah. There is no realization at all that the Muslim Ummah is now afflicted with internal and external dissension and conflict. If academic humility and inner blindness could be left behind, then the clarification of the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab would be eye-opening for this group: 'And we too are in subsidiary matters upon the madhhab of Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal, and we do not deny one who follows any one of the four Imams to the exclusion of others, because the madhhabs of others (like the Rafidah, Zaydis, Imamis, and the like) are not preserved, and we do not allow them upon the corrupt, rather we compel them to follow one of the four Imams.' (al-Durar al-Saniyya, vol. 1, p. 327) Take note of how the virtuous predecessors showed a mirror to the successors. 'Is there then anyone who will take heed?' Most of the writings on Islamic jurisprudence are directly related to the explanation of rulings. Among them, the more comprehensive and standard works have been included in the curriculum of Islamic seminaries for centuries. Among these, some books are related purely to juristic principles and rules, of which a few are very famous and widely circulated. Risalah al-Karkhi by Abu Muhsin al-Husayn al-Karkhi (d. 340 AH); Allama Najm al-Din Abu Hafs Umar ibn Ahmad al-Nasafi (d. 537 AH) added examples and evidences to it, which is printed with Ta'sis al-Nazar. Ta'sis al-Nazar by Ubayd Allah ibn Umar ibn Isa al-Abusi (d. 430 AH). Majami' al-Haqa'iq by Abu Sa'id [illegible] (d. 1176 AH). Manafi' al-Daqa'iq, a commentary on Majami' al-Haqa'iq by Mustafa ibn Muhammad al-Kawzi al-Ansari (d. 1315 AH). Al-Fara'id al-Hamiyya on al-Qawa'id wa al-Fara'id al-Fiqhiyya by Mahmud Hamza al-Khatib al-Dimashqi (d. 1305 AH). [Najm?] (d. 980 AH). This book is among the applied juristic rules, in which the application of juristic rules to issues and branches has been done so extensively and in detail that a jurist can deduce the rulings of new occurrences and events in every time and place in the light of these rules. This book is of paramount importance on its subject, therefore it is taught to students of ifta' so that they may develop the ability to deduce rulings. Due to the extraordinary importance of the book, the honorable scholar, Maulana Mufti Muhammad Mas'um Qasmi, the principal of Madrasatul Momineen, and it is unparalleled and included in the curriculum: al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Imam Zayn al-Din ibn [Abi?] Muhammad al-Shahrazuri.
Source pages p. 5

Commentary
This passage is a taqriz (introductory eulogy) written by Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, a Hadith teacher at Darul Uloom Waqf Deoband, praising the science of fiqh and defending the necessity of taqlid (following the four Imams). The author begins by extolling Islamic fiqh as a unique intellectual achievement unparalleled in any other religion. He highlights the meticulousness of the great jurists in extracting rulings from the Quran and Hadith, comparing them to bees producing pure honey. He then specifically praises Imam Abu Hanifa as the originator of Islamic fiqh and mentions his illustrious students, Qadi Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani. An anecdote is related about a Christian scholar amazed by the depth of Imam Muhammad's 'al-Mabsut'. The author then criticizes a group (apparently Ghayr Muqallids or similar) who oppose taqlid of the four Imams and follow their own desires. He argues that without following one of the four Imams, even performing wudu correctly is impossible. To support his argument, he quotes from the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab, who stated that they follow Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal in subsidiary matters and compel Muslims to follow one of the four Imams, rejecting the madhhabs of the Rafidah, Zaydis, etc. The taqriz then transitions to discussing important works on usul al-fiqh and qawaid fiqhiyya (legal maxims), listing several key texts: Risalah al-Karkhi, Ta'sis al-Nazar, Majami' al-Haqa'iq, Manafi' al-Daqa'iq, al-Fara'id al-Hamiyya, and finally the book itself, al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Imam Zayn al-Din al-Shahrazuri. The author emphasizes the importance of these books for students of ifta' to develop the ability to deduce rulings for new situations.

Key Terms
قواعد فقہیہ (qawaid fiqhiyya): Legal maxims that summarize and unify many individual rulings across different chapters of fiqh.
نوازل (nawazil): New, unprecedented events that require a ruling from qualified jurists.
تقلید (taqlid): Following one of the four recognized Imams in subsidiary matters of fiqh.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the passage, what is the main purpose of studying books like al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir?
A) To memorize all the rulings for personal practice.
B) To develop the ability to deduce rulings for new events (nawazil).
C) To critique other madhhabs.
D) To become a historian of fiqh.

Key Takeaway
The classical qawaid works, especially al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir, are the essential toolkit for muftis to derive rulings for unprecedented cases.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
8 min
The Need for Unity and the Role of Legal Maxims in Hanafi Ifta
Preface arguing for madhhab unity and introducing a commentary on legal maxims

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the purpose of Hanafi legal maxims (qawa'id fiqhiyya) and explain how a commentary on Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair aids students of ifta in deriving rulings.

Core Idea
Legal maxims empower a jurist to derive rulings for any new situation, securing unity within the Hanafi school.

This passage is the preface of a modern commentary on Ibn Nujaym's Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair, a foundational Hanafi work on legal maxims. The author stresses the urgency of intellectual unity among Muslims and refutes those who reject all madhhab adherence by citing the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab. The preface then introduces the science of qawa'id fiqhiyya and lists key classical works, culminating in the text being commented upon. The commentator's aim is to provide a clear, applied understanding of these maxims so that students of ifta can confidently deduce rulings for contemporary problems.

Guided Path
1
Identify the core problem addressed
Read the opening lament about false accusations against imams and sectarian strife. What is the author's diagnosis?
He sees disunity and deviation from the four madhhabs as a root cause.
2
Analyze the quoted rebuttal
Examine the citation from Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab's son. How does it support adherence to a madhhab?
It shows that even the Wahhabi founder insisted on following one of the four imams, rejecting free-for-all interpretation.
3
Identify the proposed solution
The author points to 'intellectual unity'. What tool does he offer to achieve this in fiqh?
He introduces the study of qawa'id fiqhiyya and specifically the commentary on Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair.
4
Trace the list of foundational works
The preface names several books. Why does the author highlight Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair as the focus?
Because it provides applied legal maxims that allow a jurist to derive rulings for any time and place.
5
Assess the commentary's pedagogy
What features of the new commentary are praised? How do they serve the student of ifta?
Vowelized translation, pleasant explanation, easy clarity—all aimed at nurturing the ability to deduce rulings.

منگلور اتراکھنڈ نے شرح لکھنے کا ارادہ کیا۔ اور الحمد للہ وہ اس میں کامیاب بھی ہوئے، ہر قاعدہ کا با اعراب سلیس ترجمہ با محاورہ ، تشریح دلنشیں اور عام فہم وضاحت، یہ ان کی اس شرح کی بنیادی خصوصیت ہے جس سے افتاء کے طلباء بخوبی مستفید ہو سکیں گے۔ عزیز موصوف اس میدان میں نو آموز نہیں ہیں، اس سے پہلے نورالایضاح جیسے جامع فقہی متن کی بہترین شرح لکھ چکے ہیں جس سے اساتذہ و طلباء یکساں طور پر مستفید ہو رہے ہیں۔ مختلف دینی موضوعات پر آسان زبان میں متعدد کتابیں ان کے صریر خامہ کے کرشموں کا ثبوت پیش کرتی ہیں۔
موصوف پختہ مدرس ہونے کے ساتھ سنجیدہ خطیب بھی ہیں ، علم و عمل کے ہر میدان میں ان کی با معنی موجودگی اس بات کا بین ثبوت ہے کہ موصوف صحیح معنی میں اسلاف کی پاکیزہ روایات کو اپنے علم عمل اور قلم سے زندہ کر رہے ہیں۔ دعاء ہے کہ اللہ رب العزت ان کی اس خدمت کو اپنی بارگاہ میں شرف قبولیت سے نوازے۔ اور پیہم خدمت کی توفیق ارزانی فرمائے۔ (آمین)
( حضرت مولانا غلام نبی کشمیری استاذ حدیث دار العلوم وقف دیوبند
False accusations are spreading against the noble imams such that even Satan would seek refuge. In some regions of India, simple Muslims are caught in such [؟] and struggle about their religion at the hands of this arbitrary and whimsical group; the worst result sometimes appears in the form of deviation from religion. This condition of obstinacy and stubbornness is such that we need the balm of intellectual unity on these wounds, not to sprinkle salt by criticizing the pillars of the community. There is no awareness that the Muslim Ummah is afflicted with internal and external discord; if they left behind academic poverty and inner blindness, then the explanation of the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab is eye-opening for this group: 'And we too in subsidiary matters follow the madhhab of Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal, and we do not deny the one who follows any of the four imams, because of the lack of control over the madhhabs of others—the Rafidis, Zaydis, Imamis, and their likes—and we will not let them follow corrupt [beliefs], rather we will force them to follow one of the four imams.' (Al-Durar al-Sunniyya, vol. 1, p. 327). See how the virtuous predecessors showed a mirror to their successors. "Is there any who will take heed?" Most of the books written on Islamic jurisprudence are directly concerned with the explanation of rulings. Among them, the more comprehensive and standard collection has been included in the curricula of Islamic seminaries for centuries. Among these, some books deal purely with fiqhi principles and rules, and several are very famous and current. Risala al-Karkhi by Abu Muhsin al-Husayn al-Karkhi (d. 340 AH); upon it, Allama Najm al-Din Abu Hafs Umar ibn Ahmad al-Nasafi (d. 537 AH) added examples and evidence, which is printed with 'Tasis al-Nazar'. Tasis al-Nazar by Ibn Zayd Ubayd Allah ibn Umar ibn Isa al-? (d. 430 AH). Majami' al-Haqa'iq by Abu Sa'id Hamd al-Mal (d. 1176 AH). Manafi' al-Daqa'iq, commentary on Majami' al-Haqa'iq by Mustafa ibn Muhammad al-Kuzi al-Ansari (d. 1315 AH). Al-Fara'id al-Hamiyya on al-Qawa'id wa al-Fara'id al-Fiqhiyya by Mahmud Hamza al-Khatib al-Dimashqi (d. 1305 AH). And Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Zayn al-Din ibn Ibrahim ibn Nujaym (d. 970 AH). This book is among the applied fiqhi rules, in which the application of fiqhi rules to issues and branches is so extensive and detailed that a jurist can deduce rulings for new occurrences and events in every time and place in the light of these rules. Due to its tremendous importance on its subject, it is taught to students of ifta so that they can develop the ability to deduce rulings. Considering the extraordinary importance of the book, the honorable scholar Maulana Mufti Muhammad Masum Qasimi, director of Madrasat al-Mu'minin, Mangalur, Uttarakhand, intended to write a commentary. And all praise is due to Allah, he succeeded in this. The basic features of this commentary are: the vowelized smooth idiomatic translation of each rule, pleasant explanation, and easy-to-understand clarification, from which students of ifta will benefit well. The respected author is not a novice in this field; before this, he has written an excellent commentary on the comprehensive fiqhi text Nur al-Idah, from which teachers and students alike are benefiting. Many books on various religious topics in easy language bear witness to the miracles of his pen. The author is a seasoned teacher as well as a serious orator. His meaningful presence in every field of knowledge and action is clear evidence that he is reviving the pure traditions of the predecessors through his knowledge, practice, and pen. Prayer that Allah Almighty bestows upon him the honor of acceptance in His court, and grants him continuous success. (Amin). (Hazrat Maulana Ghulam Nabi Kashmiri, teacher of Hadith, Darul Uloom Waqf Deoband.)
Source pages p. 6

Commentary
This passage is the preface of the commentary. It begins by lamenting the spread of false accusations against the classical imams and the sectarian strife that has afflicted Muslims, especially due to groups that reject traditional madhhab adherence. It then quotes the son of Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab to show that even the founder of the Wahhabi movement insisted on following one of the four madhhabs, contradicting those who claim total independence from them. The author points to the need for intellectual unity rather than criticism. Then it introduces the subject matter: books of Islamic jurisprudence, specifically those on usul al-fiqh and qawaid fiqhiyya. It lists several classical works, culminating in Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Ibn Nujaym, which is a foundational text on Hanafi legal maxims. The preface explains that this work is of immense importance for deriving rulings from principles, and it is taught to students of ifta. The commentator, Maulana Mufti Muhammad Masum Qasimi, has written a new commentary (sharh) on this text, providing a clear translation, pleasant explanation, and easy understanding. The preface emphasizes that the commentator is well-qualified, having previously authored a commentary on Nur al-Idah. The passage ends with praise and a prayer for acceptance of the work. This front matter orients the reader to the purpose and significance of the commentary: to produce jurists (fuqaha) who can apply qawaid to new problems.

Key Terms
قواعد فقہیہ (qawa'id fiqhiyya): Fundamental legal principles from which specific rulings are derived, forming the basis for ijtihad and fatwa.
افتاء (ifta): The process of issuing fatwas, requiring deep knowledge of legal sources and methodology.
استنباط (istinbat): Deduction of legal rulings from primary sources or principles.

Key Terms from Source Passage

D) To promote the author's previous works.

Key Takeaway
The preface establishes that mastering Hanafi legal maxims through Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair is essential for any mufti to derive rulings consistently and maintain madhhab unity.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
The Significance of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair in Hanafi Ifta
Commendation endorsing the commentary.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the importance of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair as the foundation of Hanafi legal maxims and explain why a reliable commentary is essential for students of ifta.

Core Idea
Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair is the key to mastering Hanafi qawa'id — without it, ifta is incomplete.

This taqriz introduces you to the esteemed commentary of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair, the seminal work on Hanafi legal maxims. The author of the taqriz, Maulana Abd al-Rashid Bistawi, highlights the book's unique status and the translator's accessible style. This lesson will orient you to the role of this text in your journey towards proficiency in ifta.

Guided Path
1
Identify the genre
Recognize that this is a taqriz, a formal commendation endorsing the work. Understand that it establishes the text's credibility.
Taqriz is common in Islamic scholarly tradition to introduce and validate a work.
2
Assess the status of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair
Note that the author, Ibn Nujaym, is a mujtahid fi al-madhhab, and this is a foundational text for Hanafi qawa'id.
The text is part of the curriculum for takhassus fi al-fiqh.
3
Understand the need for commentary
The original text is concise and intricate; a clear translation/commentary is crucial for students.
The taqriz mentions 'isma wa i'qad' (complexity) as a reason.
4
Evaluate the translator's contribution
Appreciate the translator's simple language and careful explanation of branches and applications.
The taqriz praises the use of vowel signs (tashkil) and easy style.
5
Connect to your studies
This commentary covers only the first 17 principles; the rest will follow, so treat this as a starting point.
The taqriz mentions remaining volumes in sha Allah.

Commendation: Hazrat Maulana Abd al-Rashid Bistawi, may his blessings endure, teacher of Hadith at Jami'a Imam Anwar Shah Deoband. Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds, and blessings and peace upon His faithful Messenger and upon all his family and companions. Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair is a highly important, unique, and distinguished book of Hanafi fiqh. The author himself is a high-ranking scholar and jurist, and in terms of the classification of jurists, he is among the mujtahid fi al-madhhab. In the entire history of fiqh, only a few such personalities have passed in all four schools of jurisprudence. 'This felicity is not by strength of arm; until the Generous God bestows.' This book, for many reasons, from the time of its composition until now, in Hanafi fiqh seminaries, has been part of the curriculum in specialization in fiqh (takhassus fi al-fiqh) and has held a distinguished position in enhancing students' analytical abilities. However, it is also true that the text of this book is concise, somewhat complex and intricate, and beyond the reach of ordinary scholars who do not possess a deep understanding. For this reason, not only has full attention been focused on its teaching and instruction, but also the need for its translation and commentary was felt. Driven by the desire to fulfill this need, my respected brother, Maulana Mufti Muhammad Mas'um, the principal of Madrasa al-Mu'minin in Manglaur, district Haridwar, undertook the service of translating and explaining this book. Previously, Mufti Sahib has authored several books on various topics and has also written a commentary on an important basic book like Nur al-Idah, which contains reliable mufti-related issues, in two volumes. Mufti Sahib's language is simple and fluent, which is the first brick for the usefulness of any Dars-e-Nizami book's translation and commentary. In this book too, Mufti Sahib paid special attention to the original text, used easy language in translation, provided charming explanations of interrelated issues of transactions, and adorned the text with correct diacritics. In this regard, Akhtar also directed attention to some useful aspects, and Mufti Sahib, like a capable scholar, accepted it with great open-mindedness. The present part consists of the translation and explanation of only seventeen principles of al-Ashbah, along with their branches and applications. The commentary of the remaining part, God willing, will be done in subsequent volumes. Given the effort Mufti Sahib has put into the commentary, the clarity with which he has explained the issues, and the excellent writing style he has adopted, the nation hopes that this commentary of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair will be well-received among the experts of fiqh and ifta in seminaries and among students of specialization in fiqh and ifta, and they will fully benefit from it. Prayer that Allah Almighty may honor this commentary with acceptance and make it easy for Mufti Sahib to perform further academic and religious writings. Amen. Humble servant, Abd al-Rashid Bistawi, Jami'a Imam Anwar Deoband. 18/4/1436.

The author praises the original work and the translator's efforts. The passage highlights the importance of al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair in Hanafi fiqh, its challenging nature, and the need for accessible commentary. It also notes that this volume covers only the first seventeen principles (al-Asl) with their furu' and applications, and the rest will follow in later volumes. The taqriz serves as an endorsement and introduction to the commentary.

Key Terms
تقريظ (taqriz): A commendation or laudatory preface written by a scholar endorsing the work and author.
الاشباه والنظائر (al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair): A seminal Hanafi work on legal maxims (qawa'id) and analogous cases, written by Zayn al-Din Ibn Nujaym.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner

Introduction to Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir and Its Commentary
Two commendations praising an Urdu commentary on Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the significance of Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir in the Hanafi ifta curriculum and explain the purpose of taqrizat as scholarly endorsements.

Core Idea
Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir is the foundational text for Hanafi legal maxims, essential for ifta training.

Before diving into the legal maxims themselves, it is important to understand the authority and purpose of the source text. This lesson introduces you to Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Ibn Nujaym, a cornerstone of Hanafi fatwa methodology, and explains how scholarly commendations (taqrizat) help establish the reliability of a commentary.

Guided Path
1
Identify the original work
Locate the name of the Arabic work being commented upon. The passage mentions 'الاشباه والنظائر' by Ibn Nujaym al-Misri. Recognize that this is a classical Hanafi text on legal maxims (qawa'id fiqhiyya).
2
Understand the purpose of taqrizat
Taqrizat are formal endorsements by respected scholars. They serve to certify the quality and reliability of a book, especially for educational use. In this passage, two scholars praise the commentary and pray for its acceptance.
Taqrizat are common in Islamic scholarly tradition, especially for new works used in madrasas.
3
Note the scope of the commentary
The first taqriz states that the present volume covers only the first seventeen principles from Al-Ashbah, with subsequent volumes planned. This helps you understand that the commentary is a multi-volume work.
4
Recognize the intended audience
Both taqrizat mention that the commentary is aimed at students of fiqh and ifta, particularly those in specialization programs. This tells you that the work is designed for advanced study of fatwa methodology.
The audience includes 'arbab fiqh wa ifta' and 'talaba shu'ba takhassus fi al-fiqh wa al-ifta'.

Commentary
This passage consists of two taqrizat (commendations) written by different scholars—Abdur Rashid Bastavi and Muhammad Yusuf—in praise of an Urdu commentary on the classical Hanafi work Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Ibn Nujaym. The first commendation highlights that the commentary covers only seventeen principles from the original, with further volumes planned. It emphasizes the commentator's effort, clarity, and writing style, expressing hope that the commentary will be widely accepted in madrasas and among students of ifta specialization. The second commendation, by Muhammad Yusuf, identifies Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir as a famous text and part of the ifta curriculum, praising Mufti Muhammad Masoom Qasmi's simple Urdu explanation and praying for its acceptance and the author's further service. These pages are introductory and establish the significance and quality of the commentary for the reader.

Key Terms
الاشباه والنظائر (Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir): A famous work by Ibn Nujaym al-Misri on Hanafi legal maxims, used as a textbook in ifta courses.
تقريظ (taqriz): A commendation or endorsement written by a scholar to praise and recommend a book.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
The Significance of Taqriz in Hanafi Scholarship
Two endorsements for an Urdu commentary on al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the role of a taqriz in Hanafi scholarly tradition and explain how it establishes the authority of a text in the ifta curriculum.

Core Idea
A taqriz by a senior scholar validates a text's reliability and situates it within the Hanafi pedagogical hierarchy.

This lesson examines two endorsements (taqriz) for an Urdu commentary on Ibn Nujaym's Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair. These endorsements are not mere praise; they serve to certify the work's usefulness and position it within the established curriculum of Ifta studies. Understanding the function of taqriz helps you appreciate how the Hanafi school preserves and transmits its legal tradition.

Guided Path
1
Identify the authors of the taqriz
Note their scholarly credentials (e.g., Mufti Muhammad Yusuf, servant of Hadith at Darul Uloom Deoband; Maulana Muhammad Shakib Qasimi).
Their positions lend weight to the endorsement.
2
Locate the text being endorsed
The text is Al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair by Ibn Nujaym, a core text in the Ifta curriculum.
The endorser explicitly states it is included in the syllabus.
3
Analyze the language of endorsement
Phrases like 'very famous book', 'easy style', and 'beneficial for students' indicate pedagogical suitability.
Highlight the value for students of ifta.
4
Determine the function of the taqriz
To recommend the book to students and confirm its alignment with Hanafi methodology.
It also serves as a scholarly chain of transmission.
5
Relate to the discipline of iftaa
The taqriz ensures that the commentary is a reliable tool for future muftis.
Without such endorsements, a text may not gain acceptance in traditional curricula.
